======== Scenario: col_necromancerlab ========
Session Sequence: AD_MintharaEntersLab -> AD_Zombie
----- Session: AD_MintharaEntersLab -----
Synopsis: 

Nightwarden Minthara: Whatever experiments Balthazar performed here, I fear he made more than thralls and ghouls.

Cal, Danis, Dror Ragzlin, GROUP_Act2_COL_NecromancerZombies, Lakrissa, Lia, Nickels, Nightwarden Minthara, Nimble, Wulbren Bongle: *Groan.* || [context] NodeContext: SFX only. zombie sound.

======== Scenario: col_memorylibrary ========
Session Sequence: PAD_Manuscripts
----- Session: PAD_Manuscripts -----
Synopsis: This dialog plays upon rolling a passive Arcana check after reading one of the illithid manuscripts in the lower Colony's Memory Library.For tadpoled companions, each companion will see this check once, after reading an illithid manuscript, unless someone else has succeeded this check.For non-tadpoled companions, a different check occurs when they try to read the illithid manuscripts. As they do not have a tadpole, they can't read the script, and will remark on this. A different Arcana Check occurs in script, and the resulting AD from this check will also play again everytime they try to read an illithid manuscript afterwards.So for non-tadpoled companions (no ILLITHID tag) this dialog is repeatable, but not for tadpoled companions.

Player: Seems I can understand illithid script. Thank you, tadpole.

: Tread carefully. That telepathic storm is now a tempest.

Narrator: *But in denial, too. It will not open, even for you.*

======== Scenario: col_kethericshowdown ========
Session Sequence: AD_Phase3Transition -> AD_NightsongApostle -> KethericIntro -> PAD_AfterCombatComment -> DaisyAD_ElderBrain -> AD_NightsongTransform -> AD_KethericInvulnerable -> AD_NightsongAfterCombat
----- Session: AD_Phase3Transition -----
Synopsis: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony, when the third phase of the fight starts, this will play only once on Ketheric when his turn starts. Ketheric, in his Apostle of Myrkul form, calls upon the Necromites to sacrifice themselves to heal him.

: UNLIFE TO MY LIFE - SUSTAIN ME, SLAVES.

----- Session: AD_NightsongApostle -----
Synopsis: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony, after Ketheric has transformed into his Apostle form/reached his second stage, Nightsong will react to this upon her first combat turn after this.

Nightsong: Now you wear a face to match your soul, oathbreaker. || [context] NodeContext: Scorn in the heat of battle - her nemesis has just turned into a hideous monster

----- Session: KethericIntro -----
Synopsis: This dialog plays at the start of the Ketheric boss fight in the Colony. There are numerous permutations here: Nightsong being dead or alive, freed from her soul cage (through stealth before being spotted); Isobel being absent or tadpoled or tadpoled and killed (in the boss chamber) before entering the dialog; Jaheira being present here (and spotted) or being absent.

Ketheric Thorm: There you are. As predicted. What is it, I wonder, that draws one toward death like a moth to light?
Ketheric Thorm: You could have run away. Absconded with the Prism - the one thing that could prevent me from fulfilling my destiny.
Ketheric Thorm: But the lure of one's destiny is irresistible, isn't it?
Ketheric Thorm: Perhaps you hoped to learn your place in history before you are erased from it. A bright flash of clarity before the snuffing-out.
Player: Why is the Prism so important to you?
Ketheric Thorm: The very fact of your being attests to its power - despite your infection, you resisted the brain, here in the heart of its domain.
Ketheric Thorm: What good is an army of thralls if they do not obey their master?
Ketheric Thorm: Let us speak plainly.
Ketheric Thorm: My Lord Myrkul gave me the one thing I desired - the one thing that no other god could grant me.
Ketheric Thorm: My daughter's life returned. Her heart beating once more.
Ketheric Thorm: For that, he asked that I serve as his Chosen, join Orin and Gortash to grow the cult of the Absolute, and then... take control of it.
Ketheric Thorm: He's never had a more devoted follower.
Ketheric Thorm: I have fought great wars before, in the service of other gods, and other powers. But for Myrkul, I would condemn all of Faern to death.
Ketheric Thorm: You are all that stands between me and my destiny - and you have brought the Prism here.
Ketheric Thorm: I will kill you now. And then I will raise you as my servant. || [context] NodeContext: Cold, merciless ire.
Player: Enough talk. Let's finish this.
Ketheric Thorm: With pleasure.

----- Session: PAD_AfterCombatComment -----
Synopsis: A PAD commenting on defeating Ketheric in his Apostle form at the end of the mind flayer Colony. After this the player will say that they need to go discuss the next course of action with their allies (alluding to Intermezzo in Moonrise Tower).At this point the players should take Ketheric's Netherstone (but we can't ensure that a player hasn't already looted said netherstone off his corpse by the time that end node is played).If there are two players available, they will banter together, otherwise a solo PAD will play.

Player: The Chosen of Myrkul is dead - permanently, this time. || [context] NodeContext: Karlach: She's distracted. More focused on Gortash.

----- Session: DaisyAD_ElderBrain -----
Synopsis: The Elder Brain. One of the cruelest and most powerful creatures that exist. Subservient to those three. And those gems seem to be the key. We must obtain them.

: An elder brain... One of the cruellest and most powerful creatures in existence, enslaved by mere mortals.

----- Session: AD_NightsongTransform -----
Synopsis: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony, after Nightsong is freed from her soul cage. She will transform into her paladin form.

Nightsong: MOONMAIDEN, HEAR ME! DAME AYLIN IS FREE! || [context] NodeContext: Scorn in the heat of battle - her nemesis has just turned into a hideous monster

----- Session: AD_KethericInvulnerable -----
Synopsis: This AD plays during the Ketheric Showdown in the lower Colony, when the player tries to damage Ketheric while he is invulnerable (Nightsong is still in the soul cage). Ketheric will react to the damage attempt. This will play if Ketheric is in his human form.

: Have you not learned? I am beyond death, fool.

----- Session: AD_NightsongAfterCombat -----
Synopsis: This dialogue will play when interacting with Nightsong after the Ketheric Showdown combat at the end of the Colony.

Nightsong: We fly at your word. || [context] NodeContext: Scorn in the heat of battle - her nemesis has just turned into a hideous monster

In this flow, the evacuation of the Colony is a lot more pressing because Ketheric was attacked.

======== Scenario: col_vault ========
Session Sequence: DaisyAD_GrandDesignReaction -> Puzzle -> PAD_GrandDesign -> AD_Solving
----- Session: DaisyAD_GrandDesignReaction -----
Synopsis: Daisy reacts to seeing an illithid sculpture of the Grand Design.

: The Grand Design. The restoration of the mind flayer empire. The dream of all illithids.

----- Session: Puzzle -----
Synopsis: This dialog plays when interacting with the button at the Colony Vault. It is an interaction with the mind within the illithid machine. Only companions with a tadpole may interact with the machine, or they will be denied access.Interacting with the mind allows the player to start solving the puzzle, reset the puzzle or talk to it after the puzzle is solved. When it is solved, the mind considers you its master, and you can ask it to do things like open or close the vaults (which contain rewards), show you a map of the Colony or "shatter" the mind to its original state.

Narrator: *As the console bursts into life, a mind touches your own. Alien and full of desperate need - but fragmented, too.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Shot of puzzle space as it winks into existence
Narrator: *It is... incomplete. It yearns to connect - but needs you to guide the process, linking each part of your mind to its like.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Shot of the starting point of the player's mind, and the ending point of the machine's, with all the unconnected paths in between.
Player: Begin to manipulate the mind.

----- Session: PAD_GrandDesign -----
Synopsis: 

Gale: I wonder, how did the Illithid Empire fall?
Karlach, Lae'zel, Shadowheart: Probably with a great gooey bang.

----- Session: AD_Solving -----
Synopsis: AD occasionally played as the player solves the puzzle, providing feedback to the player.

Mind of the Vault: Wel... Welcome back, masterrrr! || [context] InternalNodeContext: Partial lucidity (3 out of 3 brain parts activated; fully lucid in following lines as puzzle is now solved)NodeContext: Mechanically distorted speech; almost "normal"

======== Scenario: col_tadpolingcentre ========

----- Session: AD_MemoryImprint_003_Mindflayer -----
Synopsis: AD for a mind flayer's memory imprint in the Tadpoling Centre, showing who they used to be when they entered the pod.

Narrator: *The device releases a stream of fragmented memories and emotions - all that remains of the pod inhabitant's former self.*
Narrator: *Desperation... pain... terror. Cultists raided his village - he was the sole survivor.*

----- Session: AD_MemoryImprint_004_Mindflayer -----
Synopsis: AD for a memory imprint on an empty pod in the Tadpoling Centre.

Narrator: *The device does not react to your presence.*

----- Session: AD_MemoryImprint_006_Zevlor -----
Synopsis: AD for Zevlor's memory imprint in the Tadpoling Centre, showing a memory from before he was imprisoned here.

Narrator: *You remember the shattered windows of Elturel's High Cathedral, the burning black sky of Avernus beyond.*
Narrator: *In its horror, the Blood War unites you. Tiefling, dwarf and elf alike huddle behind the shields of your paladin order, waiting for salvation. But when it comes... disunity.*
Narrator: *The returned city casts your people out, the devils who dragged them down to hell. In the end, it is not your paladin oath that is broken: it is your faith itself.*

----- Session: Pods -----
Synopsis: Interacting with the mind flayer device in the Tadpoling Centre that controls the pods inside. You get to choose whether to free or purge the occupants of the pods - mind flayers and innocents alike.

Narrator: *You connect to the device, and gain control of the pods - and the fate of their occupants.*
Narrator: *The device is open to your tadpole's command - to your authority.*
Player: Purge. || [approval] ['Gale -1', 'Karlach -5', "Lae'zel 5", 'Shadowheart -5', 'Wyll 5', 'Minthara 1', 'Halsin -5']

----- Session: PostCombat_Yeva -----

----- Session: DarkUrgePod -----
Synopsis: A player character interacts with a pod in the Tadpoling Centre that once belonged to the Dark Urge character. Other player characters may also investigate the pod, and imply something about who the pod belonged to if they succeed a skill check.

Narrator: *This pod has a different air to its chitinous cavern. Dust and dirt are gathered on the inside.*
Narrator: *It's broken beyond repair. Seemingly by a blunt impact, as if whoever was inside threw themselves against it in an effort to break out.* || [context] CinematicNodeContext: Dark Urge bends down next to the pod, to look into the area beyond the glass, it doesn't have to be shown

Narrator: *These pods are made to preserve. Time means nothing.*

======== Scenario: sce_cerys ========

Shes adjusting to a life without Zevlor, and briefly reflects on his surrender and presumed death.

Cerys: And then, a blinding light cuts through the darkness, like a blade through butter. All thanks to you, I hear.
Cerys: Didn't think we'd make it without the old Hellrider to lead us. But you did a damn fine job.

Cerys: Turns out the people around him were better than him. Guess he got what was coming to him.
Player: You shouldn't speak ill of the dead - Zevlor did his best. || [approval] ['Astarion 1', 'Gale 1', "Lae'zel -1", 'Shadowheart 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Karlach 1', 'Minthara -1', 'Halsin 1']

======== Scenario: sce_wulbren ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: This dialogue is peak Wulbren. If he's met you in haven (after you saved him), he rolls back on how rude he was as he realises the player would be an amazing asset in the city. If this is your first time meeting him since the escape (if haven is destroyed he waits out on the river until this scene in the epilogue), he realises how good the player would be to have on his side in the city and tells him all about how wronged the ironhand gnomes were.

Wulbren Bongle: You helped me escape this hellspit, then took down the heart of Moonrise - Ketheric himself. I'm impressed.
Wulbren Bongle: And I'm not a man easily impressed.
Player: Last I saw you, you were disappearing on a boat down the river.
Wulbren Bongle: Not my finest exit. I hid out on the river until the sky lit up. Couldn't believe my eyes - especially when I realised you were behind it. || [context] NodeContext: sincere and impressed
Wulbren Bongle: I underestimated you. Kept who I was, and who I represent, from you - but I see now that was a mistake.
Wulbren Bongle: I am Wulbren Bongle, leader of the Ironhand Gnomes. No doubt you've heard of us? || [context] NodeContext: said with immense pride
: True
Narrator: *You recall stories of the Ironhand Gnomes - a talented group of inventors who were banished from Baldur's Gate.*
Player: I don't know much, I'm afraid.
Wulbren Bongle: We are inventors of the highest order, matched, perhaps, but never surpassed by the Gondians at the High House of Wonders.
Wulbren Bongle: But our forebears were foolish - complicit with Sarevok's madness over a century past, and so we were banished. Still are to this day.
Player: Pity he never succeeded. || [approval] ['Astarion 1']
Wulbren Bongle: You agree with such machinations? Duly noted.
Wulbren Bongle: I've fought tooth and nail to restore our reputation. Particularly against Gondian detractors who live in glass houses.
Wulbren Bongle: I've filled appeals - pleaded with the High Artificer himself. They've refused us time and again. Now, however, I will make them listen.
Player: Good luck with that.
Wulbren Bongle: Our cause is just and righteous, friend. That's all the luck we need. || [context] NodeContext: determined and zealous

======== Scenario: sce_halsin ========
Session Sequence: 
----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: Dialogue with Halsin in the epilogue of Act 2. In it, he reacts to the various states that could occur in relation to his desire to rid the Act 2 region of the shadow curse:- if you've already done everything needed to ensure success. he's grateful and seeks to remain with you on the journey to Baldur's Gate.- if the curse is not yet sure to be lifted, but there's still something that can be done (ie Thaniel was saved from the Shadowfell, but hasn't been fully restored), he will implore the players to help and offer to join them.- if it's no longer possible to lift the curse, Halsin is sad and resigned to staying behind to stand sentry over it. He will not be available as a companion in Act 3, and his story effectively ends here.

Halsin: Thaniel rests still, but it's no easy slumber. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: The shadows rended him in two when they bore him away to the Shadowfell. Half of his essence remained here, amidst the curse. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: What stayed behind would have been the strongest part of him. But after all these years left in darkness, corruption must have taken hold. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Player: Can it be undone?
Halsin: Perhaps - if we can find Thaniel's lost half, and make him whole again. || [context] NodeContext: Concerned/Urgent. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Halsin: Only, the missing half may not come willingly. The curse will have sunk its tendrils deep, twisting Thaniel's essence into something... else. || [context] NodeContext: Some foreboding. The curse will not be lifted unless a spirit of the land is fully restored
Player: All right, leave it to me. || [approval] ['Astarion -1', 'Gale 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Karlach 1', 'Halsin 10']
Halsin: This doesn't have to be your burden alone. Every moment counts, and I've asked much of you already without being at your side. || [context] NodeContext: Stalwart, heartfelt
Halsin: If you want me, I'm yours. Against the curse, against the Absolute - anything. Just say the word. || [context] NodeContext: Stalwart, heartfelt
Player: Join me.
Halsin: Good. Now our roots can deepen - together. || [context] NodeContext: Resolute/comradely || [approval] ['Gale 1', 'Shadowheart 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Karlach 1']

======== Scenario: hav_siege ========

Synopsis: SCL Haven: Isobel is kidnapped/killed and shadows engulf the inn, combat starts against the shadows. At some point a huge tentacle emerges from the fountain in the middle of the yard, destroying the fountain. Player character has a PAD comment on the event.

Player: What in the hells is that? || [context] NodeContext: a giant tentacle has sprung up out of a fountain in the middle of a fight. Shock and perhaps a little furstration as player now has to fight it.

----- Session: Outro -----
Synopsis: After the battle against the shadows is over, we speak with Jaheira again. Either she hates us because she knows we killed Isobel, or she's contemplative in the aftermath of the battle, and we can have her join our camp.

[desc] 
Jaheira: It is abominable that you still live - you who has cost us so much. The murderer of light. || [context] CinematicNodeContext: (Cine) Jaheira eyes us with hatred. Shes breathing heavily, exhausted by combat against the shadow creatures. She looks down - but shes not out.NodeContext: Shes exhausted from combat, but her hatred of us keeps her standing.
Jaheira: These dead need not be buried. Beneath this canopy of darkness, all is one yard of restless graves.
Jaheira: You will lie and rot among them. || [context] NodeContext: Fiery, spat at the player
Player: You're weak; exhausted. Walk away while you still can.
: False
Jaheira: No. To let you live would be beyond cowardice. You sowed these many dead - now I will do the reaping.

Session Sequence: AD_WithGuard001
----- Session: AD_WithGuard001 -----
Synopsis: A patrolling guard stops and reports to Z'rell.

Zealot Bennel: All quiet, Disciple.
Disciple Z'rell: All quiet? Do you suppose the Absolute's enemies are resting, soldier? || [context] NodeContext: Suddenly cutting, questioning - poking at her underling's complacency.
Zealot Bennel: I - no, Disciple. || [context] NodeContext: Taken aback at her ferocity
Disciple Z'rell: Perhaps you cannot find them - root them out - because they are your allies? Hm? || [context] NodeContext: Doubling down, demanding answers
Zealot Bennel: I - no, mistress! I  would never - || [context] NodeContext: Close to pleading - is cut off by Z'rell at the end.

----- Session: Ketheric -----
Synopsis: Evil route. Captured Nightsong

Ketheric Thorm: He had... everything. A wonderful wife. A brilliant daughter. They lived not far from here.
Ketheric Thorm: His wife died too young. Grief tore through their home like a thief, snatching away the scent of her hair, the rustle of her skirts. But the man did not break.
Ketheric Thorm: He could not break. His daughter needed him whole, after all.
Ketheric Thorm: She grew up - grew strong. Challenged him. Filled his heart with such joy it supplanted all sorrow.

Ketheric Thorm: First, he sold himself to the goddess of loss. But the pain did not subside, no matter his obscene feats of devotion.
Ketheric Thorm: Then a new god came - a god who promised the man something wonderful: his daughter. Her life returned. Imagine it.
Ketheric Thorm: He would have to give everything: his body and soul entire. He did not hesitate. Not for a moment.
Ketheric Thorm: And the new god did as promised. The man's brilliant, beautiful daughter came back. She was whole - she was alive. But she despised the pitiful wretch her father had become.
Ketheric Thorm: Her hatred he could bear, perhaps, as long as she had another chance to live.
Ketheric Thorm: Everything I've done, everything I have built, has been to give Isobel that chance. And you, True Soul - you have squandered it.
Player: You brought her back once. Do it again.

Ketheric Thorm: I have no mercy left in me - but it is for the Absolute to decide your fate. || [context] NodeContext: Almost sarcastic, like a very annoyed child talking to their parent

======== Scenario: moo_oubliette ========

----- Session:  -----

Lann Tarv: If you have coin, then show it. || [context] NodeContext: suspicious, weighing up the person he's greeting

If they failed to impresse him, he will taunt them. If not of the players attempted to impress him, he will be existed for the bloodshed regardless.

Lann Tarv: A little fun at last. || [context] NodeContext: Entering combat with relish - he was extremely bored

======== Scenario: moo_mintharafate ========
Session Sequence: AD_TorturersPostTorture -> AD_TorturersBeforeTorture -> Escaped -> AD_Torture
----- Session: AD_TorturersPostTorture -----
Synopsis: Torture scene with Minthara and her torturers is over. This dialog holds two variants, the variant where Minthara is present, therefore she's been pacified mentally and is now an obedient soldier. The other variant is the one where players take over and make the torturers leave by faking that Minthara's pacified.

Questioner Jasin: Soon, we will be in Baldur's Gate. What say you to that, sister?
Questioner Sumera: A whole city in service of the Absolute - it will be glorious.
Questioner Jasin: And so many minds for us to break.

----- Session: AD_TorturersBeforeTorture -----
Synopsis: Torturers are waiting in their room. Minthara may or may never arrive depending on story permutations. They discuss about work regardless.

Questioner Jasin: The General has descended from his chapel.
Questioner Sumera: To mete out the Absolute's justice, I hear.
Questioner Jasin: I wish we could go upstairs to watch.

----- Session: Escaped -----
Synopsis: Minthara has escaped Moonrise with the players. She is grateful and offers to move to the player camp.

Nightwarden Minthara: I last left Moonrise as a commander in the Absolute's army, obeying the voice of a god. I thought I had found a home... and a purpose. || [context] NodeContext: Looking up at the tower we just escaped, speaking with general disgust

Narrator: *The artefact connects with her, pulling your minds together, and showing her all that you have seen.*
Narrator: *The Prism, your dream visitor, the protection that keeps you from obeying the Absolute, and becoming illithid. She knows it all in a moment.*
Narrator: *Her mind reels, but is no longer clouded. She accepts the truth... she has no choice.*
Nightwarden Minthara: There is much we must discuss. Do you have a safe place to camp nearby?
Player: Tell her where to find your camp. || [approval] ['Astarion 1', "Lae'zel 1", 'Gale 1', 'Shadowheart 1', 'Karlach 1', 'Minthara 5']
Nightwarden Minthara: Goodbye for now. I will see you soon. || [context] NodeContext: Sunny and charming

----- Session: AD_Torture -----
Synopsis: Torturers are breaking Minthara.

Nightwarden Minthara: Queen of Spiders, I beseech of you the strength to destroy my foes. || [context] NodeContext: quiet, subdued prayer
Questioner Sumera: Lolth cannot hear you. She has forsaken you.
Questioner Jasin: There are no gods left to you, Minthara. You are alone.

======== Scenario: scl_halsin ========
Session Sequence: StayInSCL
----- Session: StayInSCL -----
Synopsis: Halsin tells the player his business is in SCL now and he will not leave.

Halsin: I cannot venture back with you - now that I am in a position to fight the curse, I must stay here and see it through. || [context] NodeContext: Some urgency. Halsin doesn't want to backtrack to previous regions while he's close to achieving his goals.
Player: What if I need you by my side?
Halsin: If you truly need to retread your steps, then you will have little need for me there. You are more formidable than anything that lies in our wake. || [context] NodeContext: Complimentary/'don't sell yourself short'
Halsin: I must continue to investigate the curse - this may be my last chance. I shall await your return when you are ready to continue. || [context] NodeContext: Imploring

======== Scenario: scl_oliversdiary ========
Session Sequence: PAD_HideAndSeek -> OliverShadow -> AD_CreepyNoises -> AD_OliverDeathScream
----- Session: PAD_HideAndSeek -----
Synopsis: AD played when the player finds or fails to find Oliver during hide & seek.

Player: Where'd that child go? Or... whatever it is. || [context] NodeContext: Stumped, looking for Oliver Found Oliver (a little shadow/phantom boy they're playing hide and seek with)

----- Session: OliverShadow -----
Synopsis: Dialog with Oliver, the shadow-child in the Shadowcursed Lands. Oliver wishes for the player to be his playmate, and engages in a game of hide and seek. Oliver seems to be a soul trapped by the curse for a 100 years, but the player will gradually realise over the course of the act that he is in fact a shadow version of Thaniel, the spirit of the land. Oliver possesses Thaniel's heart, and the curse cannot be lifted until it is returned. Oliver does not want to do this - he's made his own little 'family' using cursed beings in the area. If the player challenges him about Thaniel, Oliver will flee towards the town square, where a final confrontation will take place.

Oliver: You weren't supposed to find me. You weren't supposed to win. || [context] NodeContext: More confused than angry, like the impossible has happened.
Player: Don't be a sore loser.
Oliver: You're not my mummy or my daddy - don't tell me what to do.
Oliver: Let's play another game - I deserve a chance to even the score.
Player: Let's play.
Oliver: Try to find me again - but my family will be looking for you at the same time, so don't get caught! || [context] NodeContext: Excited || [approval] ['Gale 1', 'Shadowheart 1', 'Wyll 1', 'Karlach 1', 'Halsin -1']

----- Session: AD_CreepyNoises -----
Synopsis: As the player approaches the abandoned house, they hear strange noises from inside, as if someone still lived there.

Oliver: Someone's coming. Someone new. Maybe they want to play. || [context] NodeContext: Hushed anticipation. Little giggle at the end.

----- Session: AD_OliverDeathScream -----
Synopsis: Death-scream of Oliver in the Oliver's Diary booster.

Oliver: Mummy! Daddy! Betsy! No - don't leave me! || [context] NodeContext: Distraught cry

======== Scenario: sha_orthon ========
Session Sequence: AD -> AD_FormLines -> AD_TransitionsToSecondPhase -> AD_DisplacerGrowl -> 
----- Session: AD -----
Synopsis: The Orthon mumble-sings to himself while idle in his lair in the Shar Temple. Occasionally he interrupts the lyrics with frustrated outbursts.This occurs after the ambush scene, where we learn that the song is his contract, and will remain stuck in his head until he fulfills the terms.

Yurgir: Silence all prayers; smother each rite... blasted song! || [context] NodeContext: Singing to himself, with an exasperated outburst at the end

----- Session: AD_FormLines -----
Synopsis: Orthon tells the merregons to get close to him during combat.

Yurgir: Form up ranks! Don't let anything get past you! || [context] NodeContext: During combat. Bellowing orders to his merregon soldiers to change formation

----- Session: AD_TransitionsToSecondPhase -----
Synopsis: During combat, the orthon escalates to phase two (intensifying his attacks and changing up his tactics). This is prompted by:- killing a certain number of minions- lowering his HP a certain amount- surviving for a certain number of combat rounds

Yurgir: Bravo - that almost stung. Perhaps I'll make a merregon of you, once you're dead. || [context] NodeContext: Pronuncation: mer-eh-gone. Taunting, during combat. The player has injured the Orthon, who responds by changing up his tactics after this utterance.

----- Session: AD_DisplacerGrowl -----
Synopsis: The Displacer beast growls at the player if the player gets too close to it while it is in its idle behaviour if the Orthon is not hostile to the player.

Displacer Beast: *Growl.* || [context] InternalNodeContext: SFX only. Displacer growl.NodeContext: SFX only. Displacer growl.

----- Session:  -----
Synopsis: This occurs if the player has successfully convinced the orthon to let them stay in his lair. They did so by telling him they'd search the temple for a way of freeing him from his contract.If the player resolves the Last Justiciar contract, they can inform Yurgir. If they killed the justiciar, Raphael will appear and negotiate with Yurgir. If the player spared the justiciar, they can confront and fight Yurgir.

Yurgir: The song remains. Seems you haven't dealt with this imaginary Justiciar of yours. || [context] NodeContext: Impatient growl
Player: I know what you're feeding that displacer charm potions. Curious way of ensuring the beast's loyalty.
Yurgir: Curious? No - effective. A hunter needs to ensure his tools are dependable.
Yurgir: Ensuring Nessa's loyalty is as important as having sharpened blades and an oiled crossbow.
Player: You're manipulating that creature.
Yurgir: Yes. Your point? || [context] NodeContext: Deadpan.
Player: It's wrong - even a beast like that shouldn't be treated in such a way. || [approval] ['Shadowheart 1', 'Halsin 1']
Yurgir: Treated like what? Pampered? Fed? Given a master to adore?
Yurgir: Spare me your bleeding heart. Unless you'd like me to pluck it out and show it to you.
Player: Not at all. I think I'll make short work of this - show you how it's done. || [context] InternalNodeContext: Local flag unsets when the player acknowledges the Orthon's query in N200
Yurgir: Remember you said that, when you fail. You won't smile so easily when I peel the face off your skull. || [context] NodeContext: Vicious. Chaffing at the player's bravado.

Narrator: *He devoted months to formulating a deadly poison with the remaining ingredients, without success.*

Narrator: *The petals of a corpse rose.*
Narrator: *The book's index reveals corpse roses may grow near tombs, mausoleums, and particularly redolent cadavers.*
Narrator: *Thisobald enlisted a courier from Baldur's Gate to obtain corpse rose petals and other ingredients and deliver them to a covert location.*

: True
Narrator: *Your mind separates the black from the blue, revealing the stash's location. You mark your map as a reminder.*
Narrator: *With the corpse rose petals the package contains, you might create Thisobald's purple worm poison.*
